
```sql
  CREATE TABLE "T_CUSTOMERS" 
   (	"CUSTOMER_ID" NUMBER GENERATED BY DEFAULT ON NULL AS IDENTITY MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999999999999999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 CACHE 20 NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  NOT NULL ENABLE, 
	"NAME" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"ADDRESS" VARCHAR2(100), 
	"CITY" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"STATE" VARCHAR2(50), 
	"ZIPCODE" VARCHAR2(10), 
	"EMAIL" VARCHAR2(100), 
	"PHONE" VARCHAR2(20), 
	 PRIMARY KEY ("CUSTOMER_ID")
  USING INDEX  ENABLE
   ) ;

```

INSERT INTO t_customers (name, address, city, state)
SELECT name, address, city, state
FROM (
    SELECT 'Name 12' AS name, '123 Fake Street Apt 12' AS address, 'City 12' AS city, 'State 12' AS state FROM dual UNION ALL
    SELECT 'Name 13', '123 Fake Street Apt 13', 'City 13', 'State 13' FROM dual UNION ALL
    SELECT 'Name 14', '123 Fake Street Apt 14', 'City 14', 'State 14' FROM dual UNION ALL
    SELECT 'Name 15', '123 Fake Street Apt 15', 'City 15', 'State 15' FROM dual UNION ALL
    SELECT 'Name 16', '123 Fake Street Apt 16', 'City 16', 'State 16' FROM dual UNION ALL

Function and Global Variable Declaration

```js
var customerData;

function exportCustomers() {
    apex.server.process(
        'GET_CUSTOMERS_TABLE_DATA',                           
        {}, 
        {
            success: function (pData) {     
                customerData = parseCSV(pData);
                generateCustomerExcel();
            },
            dataType: "text"                     
        }
    );        
}

function parseCSV(str) {
    var arr = [];
    var quote = false;
    for (var row = 0, col = 0, c = 0; c < str.length; c++) {
        var cc = str[c], nc = str[c+1];
        arr[row] = arr[row] || [];
        arr[row][col] = arr[row][col] || '';
        if (cc == '"' && quote && nc == '"') { arr[row][col] += cc; ++c; continue; }
        if (cc == '"') { quote = !quote; continue; }
        if (cc == ',' && !quote) { ++col; continue; }
        if (cc == '\r' && nc == '\n' && !quote) { ++row; col = 0; ++c; continue; }
        if (cc == '\n' && !quote) { ++row; col = 0; continue; }
        if (cc == '\r' && !quote) { ++row; col = 0; continue; }
        arr[row][col] += cc;
    }
    return arr;
}

function textToWidth(text) {
    var ret = {};
    try {
        ret.h = (text.match(/\n/g) || []).length * 20;
        var arr = text.split("\n");
        var maxlength = 0;
        for (x in arr) {
            if (arr[x].length > maxlength) maxlength = arr[x].length;
        }
        ret.w = maxlength;
    } catch (error) {
        console.log(text);
        console.log(error);
    }
    return ret.w;
}

function colFit(sheet, rowStart, rowEnd, colStart, colEnd) {
    let colLengths = [];
    for (var col = colStart; col <= colEnd; col++) {
        var maxColLength = 0;
        for (var row = rowStart; row <= rowEnd; row++) {
            var address = XLSX.utils.encode_cell({c:col,r:row});            
            var cell = sheet[address];
            try {
                if (cell && cell.v) {
                    var length = textToWidth(cell.v);
                    if (length > maxColLength) maxColLength = length;
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.log('address not found: ' + address);
                console.log(error);
            }
        }
        colLengths[col] = {width:maxColLength};
    }
    sheet['!cols'] = colLengths;
}

function applyStyleToRange(sheet, style, range) {
    for (var col = range.s.c; col <= range.e.c; col++) {
        for (var row = range.s.r; row <= range.e.r; row++) {
            var address = XLSX.utils.encode_cell({c:col,r:row});
            var cell = sheet[address];
            if (cell) {
                cell.s = style;
            } else {
                cell = {t:"s", v:"", s: style};
            }
            sheet[address] = cell;
            if (cell.t == "z") {
                cell.t = "s";
                cell.v = "";
            }
        }
    }    
}


function setCellStyle(sheet, row, col, style) {
    const cellRef = XLSX.utils.encode_cell({r: row, c: col});
    if (!sheet[cellRef]) sheet[cellRef] = {};
    sheet[cellRef].s = Object.assign({}, sheet[cellRef].s || {}, style);
}

function applyStyleToRange(sheet, style, range) {
    for (var col = range.s.c; col <= range.e.c; col++) {
        for (var row = range.s.r; row <= range.e.r; row++) {
            setCellStyle(sheet, row, col, style);
        }
    }    

}
   

function generateCustomerExcel() {
    const workbook = XLSX.utils.book_new();
    const thinBorder = { style: "thin", color: { rgb: "000000" } };
    const thickBorder = { style: "medium", color: { rgb: "000000" } };
    const borderFull = { 
        top: thickBorder, 
        bottom: thickBorder, 
        left: thickBorder, 
        right: thickBorder 
    };
    const borderThin = { 
        top: thinBorder, 
        bottom: thinBorder, 
        left: thinBorder, 
        right: thinBorder 
    };

    // Add header row
    const headers = ["CUSTOMER_ID", "NAME", "ADDRESS", "CITY", "STATE", "ZIPCODE", "EMAIL", "PHONE"];
    let data = [headers].concat(customerData);

    // Create sheet
    let sheet = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet(data);

    // Add title
    XLSX.utils.sheet_add_aoa(sheet, [["Customer Data Export"]], {origin: "A1"});
    sheet["A1"].s = {
        font: { sz: 24, bold: true },
        alignment: { horizontal: "center", vertical: "center" }
    };

    // Merge cells for title
    sheet["!merges"] = [{ s: { r: 0, c: 0 }, e: { r: 0, c: 7 } }];

    // Apply styles
    var dim = XLSX.utils.decode_range(sheet['!ref']);

    // Header style
    var headerStyle = { 
        border: borderFull, 
        alignment: { vertical: "center", horizontal: "center", wrapText: true }, 
        fill: { fgColor: { rgb: "C0C0C0" } }, 
        font: { bold: true }
    };
    applyStyleToRange(sheet, headerStyle, {s:{r:1,c:0},e:{r:1,c:dim.e.c}});

    // Data cell style
    var dataStyle = { 
        border: borderThin, 
        alignment: { vertical: "top", wrapText: true }
    };
    applyStyleToRange(sheet, dataStyle, {s:{r:2,c:0},e:{r:dim.e.r,c:dim.e.c}});

    // Set outer borders
    for (let col = 0; col <= dim.e.c; col++) {
        setCellStyle(sheet, 1, col, { top: thickBorder });
        setCellStyle(sheet, dim.e.r, col, { bottom: thickBorder });
    }
    for (let row = 1; row <= dim.e.r; row++) {
        setCellStyle(sheet, row, 0, { left: thickBorder });
        setCellStyle(sheet, row, dim.e.c, { right: thickBorder });
    }

    // Set column widths
    sheet['!cols'] = [
        {wch: 15}, // CUSTOMER_ID
        {wch: 20}, // NAME
        {wch: 30}, // ADDRESS
        {wch: 15}, // CITY
        {wch: 20}, // STATE
        {wch: 10}, // ZIPCODE
        {wch: 25}, // EMAIL
        {wch: 20}  // PHONE
    ];

    // Set row height for title and header
    sheet['!rows'] = [
        { hpt: 30 },  // Set height for the first row (title)
        { hpt: 25 }   // Set height for the second row (header)
    ];

     // Add autofilter
    sheet['!autofilter'] = { ref: `A2:H${dim.e.r}` };


    XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(workbook, sheet, "Customer Data");
    
    XLSX.writeFile(workbook, 'Customer_Data_Export.xlsx', {compression: true});
}






```

Export Download Process 2 > Export button > Dynamic Actions > New > True > Execute JS Code

 ```js
exportCustomers()
```
